initialize() {

	// define a constant K for the population size, used below
	defineConstant("K", 32000);

	// set an mutation rate (per base position per generation) *this is specific to PTC mutations as this model does not simulate other mutations
	initializeMutationRate(1.51e-10);
	
// define a "mutation type" consisting of neutral mutations(a fixed or "f" distribution of fitness effects or DFE, with selection coefficient 0.0 and dominance coefficient 0.5)
	initializeMutationType("m1", 0.5, "f", 0.0);    // de novo PTCs
	initializeMutationType("m2", 0.5, "f", 0.0);    // standing PTCs
	m1.convertToSubstitution = F;
	m2.convertToSubstitution = F;
        m1.mutationStackPolicy = "f";  // once a PTC has occurred in a genome another PTC cannot occur in the same place

// define a "genomic element type" that uses mutation type m1, representing genomic regions that can incur de novo PTCs
	initializeGenomicElementType("g1", m1, 1.0);
	

	// define a "genomic element" for each exon on the chromosome
	initializeGenomicElement(g1, 9880, 9924);
initializeGenomicElement(g1, 10359, 10496);

// Divergence of cave populations from their phylogenetically closest surface population likely occurred between ~161 and 191 k generations ago - give model output after 175k generations
// Sample 19 random individuals from the population and output their genomes

175000 late() {
allIndividuals = sim.subpopulations.individuals;
sampledIndividuals = sample(allIndividuals, 19);
sampledIndividuals.genomes.output();
}
